They are designed to provide a hassle-free operation, increase the efficiency of the farming operation and be serviceable </div><div><br></div><div>          Our equipment is compatible with most seed trays in the market, some of the brands we support are <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20231031213120/https://containerwise.co.uk/" rel="nofollow">Containerwise</a>, <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20231031213120/https://www.garlandproducts.com/" rel="nofollow">Garland</a>, <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20231031213120/https://www.proptek.com/" rel="nofollow">Proptek</a>, <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20231031213120/https://www.modiform.com/en/" rel="nofollow">Modiform</a>, etc...
